       2             :  * @file arch/x86/disassemble.c
       3             :  *
       4             :  * @brief x86 ISA disassembler
       5             :  *
       6             :  * This is an x86 ISA disassembler. The disassembly (which is table-based)
       7             :  * extracts every possible information from an instruction, given a
       8             :  * pointer to it.
       9             :  *
      10             :  * This is a complete disassembler until SSE2 instructions. Newer
      11             :  * instructions support is far from complete. Although it has been
      12             :  * extensively tested (it has correctly disassembled the Linux kernel and
      13             :  * Photoshop), it is extremely possible that some bugs are hidden somewhere.
